## Archived Ethan Postprocessing Queue

Queue rules:

- An agent may claim only one queue row at a time.
- Before starting work on a row, the agent must change its role column to `running`, fill in the owner column, and add a timestamp plus short note in `Notes`.
- If an agent is actively working a row, the board must literally say `running` in that role column.
- `AGENT-058` always claims the highest row with `Plotting = queued`.
- `AGENT-062` may claim only the lowest queued plotting row when explicitly opened by the coordinator for a bounded disjoint parallel slice.
- When plotting finishes, set `Plotting = done` and change `Analysis` from `waiting-on-plotting` to `queued`.
- `AGENT-059` owns the top-down writer lane for priorities `4-8` and always claims the highest-priority queued analysis row within that slice.
- `AGENT-069` owns the bottom-up writer lane for priorities `9-13` and always claims the highest-numbered queued analysis row within that slice, starting at `13` and moving upward.
- When analysis finishes, set `Analysis = done` and change `Review` from `waiting-on-analysis` to `queued`.
- `AGENT-057` always claims the highest row with `Review = queued`.
- When review passes, set `Review = reviewed`.
- If review finds a real defect, do not silently patch it in review. Set `Review = blocked`, write a one-line blocker note in `Notes`, and insert a repair row immediately above the blocked run before any downstream row advances.
- After finishing a row, each agent must immediately scan the queue and self-prompt into the next eligible row inside its assigned slice.
- `campaign_synthesis` must remain `Plotting = waiting-on-all-runs-reviewed` until the first 13 rows are all `Review = reviewed`.
- Once the first 13 rows are all reviewed, `AGENT-057` changes `campaign_synthesis` to `Plotting = queued`, which re-enables the same plotting -> analysis -> review sequence for the campaign-level package.
